proc fac(in x; out y) {
  y = 1;
  while (x > 0) 
  {
    y = y * x;
    x = x - 1;
  }
}

proc swap(in x1, x2; out y1, y2) {
  y1 = x2;
  y2 = x1;
}

proc nonsense(in a, h; out b, c, d, f) {
  {
    if (a == 36)
    {
      b = 60;
      c = 2;
      d = 10;
    }
    else
    {
      b = 45;
      d = 5;
    }
    while (b > 10) 
    {
      b = b - c;
      b = b - d;
    }
  }
  if (true)
  {
    if (h == 1)
    f = 10;
    else
    f = 0;
  }
  else
  f = 10;
}
